*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Supported languages

Run R code

Use the `runCode`/`run_code` method to run R code inside the sandbox. You’ll need to pass the `language` parameter with value `r`.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sbx = await Sandbox.create()
    const execution = await sbx.runCode('print("Hello, world!")', { language: 'r' })
    console.log(execution)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.2/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.2/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[E2B Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=b46f99ca671d766158b23ca43e300829)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=fe02861017e93b6ad520ee0427c429ed)](https://e2b.dev/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Supported languages

Run Java code

Use the `runCode`/`run_code` method to run Java code inside the sandbox. You’ll need to pass the `language` parameter with value `java`.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sbx = await Sandbox.create()
    const execution = await sbx.runCode('System.out.println("Hello, world!");', { language: 'java' })
    console.log(execution)

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.1/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.1/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.1/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.8.0/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.8.0/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.8.0/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.8.0/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxID]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#options)

*   `-a, --all: kill all running sandboxes`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

spawn sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.1/sandbox#options-3)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

------------------------------------------------------------------------

[e2b sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

work with sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#usage)

    e2b sandbox [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox connect](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-connect)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all running sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxID]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#options)

*   `-a, --all: kill all running sandboxes`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

spawn sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.7/sandbox#options-3)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#usage-4)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#usage-5)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#e2b-template-publish)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

publish sandbox template

CopyCopied!

*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxID]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

spawn sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#options-3)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.1/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#usage-4)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#usage-5)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#e2b-template-publish)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

publish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#usage-6)

    e2b template publish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#options-5)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

unpublish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#usage-7)

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.3/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.3/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.3/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.3/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.3/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.3/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.3/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[E2B Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=b46f99ca671d766158b23ca43e300829)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=fe02861017e93b6ad520ee0427c429ed)](https://e2b.dev/)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

MCP Gateway

Custom Servers

In addition to the 200+ pre-built MCP servers from the [Docker MCP Catalog](https://hub.docker.com/mcp)
, you can run custom MCP servers directly from public GitHub repositories.

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-servers#how-it-works)

How it works
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you specify a GitHub repository, E2B will:

1.  Clone the repository into the sandbox
2.  Run the `installCmd` (optional) to install dependencies
3.  Run the `runCmd` to start the MCP server with stdio transport

The `runCmd` must start an MCP server that follows the [MCP specification](https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2025-06-18)
 and communicates via stdio (standard input/output).

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-servers#using-a-custom-mcp-server)

Using a custom MCP server
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import Sandbox from 'e2b'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create({
        mcp: {
            'github/modelcontextprotocol/servers': {
                installCmd: 'npm install',
                runCmd: 'sudo npx -y @modelcontextprotocol/server-filesystem /root',
            },
        },
    });
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-servers#configuration)

Configuration
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-servers#param-install-cmd)

installCmd

string

Optional command to run before starting the MCP server. Use this to install dependencies (e.g., `npm install`, `pip install -r requirements.txt`).

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-servers#param-run-cmd)

runCmd

string

required

Command to start the MCP server. Must launch a stdio-enabled MCP server.

**Important for npx-based servers:** Always include `installCmd: 'npm install'` (or equivalent) when using `npx` in your `runCmd`. Without installing dependencies first, npx will try to use the local repository and fail.

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-servers#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your custom MCP server doesn’t work as expected:

1.  Explore the sandbox either via the [dashboard](https://e2b.dev/dashboard)
     or by connecting to it via `e2b connect <sandbox-id>`
2.  Check the gateway log file with `sudo cat /var/log/mcp-gateway/gateway.log`.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/e2b-dev/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/docs/mcp/custom-servers)

[Previous](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-templates)
[ExamplesExample projects using MCP servers in E2B sandboxes\
\
Next](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/examples)

# Documentation - E2B

[E2B Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=b46f99ca671d766158b23ca43e300829)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=fe02861017e93b6ad520ee0427c429ed)](https://e2b.dev/)

⌘K

Navigation

Filesystem

Read & write files

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/read-write#reading-files)

Reading files
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can read files from the sandbox filesystem using the `files.read()` method.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    const fileContent = await sandbox.files.read('/path/to/file')
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/read-write#writing-single-files)

Writing single files
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can write single files to the sandbox filesystem using the `files.write()` method.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    
    await sandbox.files.write('/path/to/file', 'file content')
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/read-write#writing-multiple-files)

Writing multiple files
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also write multiple files to the sandbox.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    
    await sandbox.files.write([\
        { path: '/path/to/a', data: 'file content' },\
        { path: '/another/path/to/b', data: 'file content' }\
    ])

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all running sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxID]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#options)

*   `-a, --all: kill all running sandboxes`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

spawn sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.0/sandbox#options-3)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.0/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.9.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.9/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.9/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.9/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`

Navigation

Filesystem

Download data from sandbox

You can download data from the sandbox using the `files.read()` method.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import fs from 'fs'
    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    
    // Read file from sandbox
    const content = await sandbox.files.read('/path/in/sandbox')
    // Write file to local filesystem
    fs.writeFileSync('/local/path', content)
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/download#download-with-pre-signed-url)

Download with pre-signed URL
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes, you may want to let users from unauthorized environments, like a browser, download files from the sandbox. For this use case, you can use pre-signed URLs to let users download files securely. All you need to do is create a sandbox with the `secure: true` option. A download URL will then be generated with a signature that allows only authorized users to access files. You can optionally set an expiration time for the URL so that it will be valid only for a limited time.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import fs from 'fs'
    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    // Start a secured sandbox (all operations must be authorized by default)
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create(template, { secure: true })
    
    // Create a pre-signed URL for file download with a 10 second expiration
    const publicUrl = await sandbox.downloadUrl(
      'demo.txt', {
        useSignatureExpiration: 10_000, // optional
      },
    )
    
    // Download a file with a pre-signed URL (this can be used in any environment, such as a browser)
    const res = await fetch(publicUrl)
    const content = await res.text()

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

MCP Gateway

Overview

E2B provides a batteries-included MCP gateway that runs inside sandboxes, giving you type-safe access to 200+ MCP tools from the [Docker MCP Catalog](https://hub.docker.com/mcp)
 or [custom MCPs](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-servers)
 through a unified interface. This integration gives developers instant access to tools like [Browserbase](https://www.browserbase.com/)
, [Exa](https://exa.ai/)
, [Notion](https://www.notion.so/)
, [Stripe](https://stripe.com/)
, or [GitHub](https://github.com/)
. The [Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://modelcontextprotocol.io/docs/getting-started/intro)
 is an open standard for connecting AI models to external tools and data sources. E2B sandboxes provide an ideal environment for running MCP tools, giving AI full access to an internet-connected Linux machine where it can safely install packages, write files, run terminal commands, and AI-generated code.

![](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/JsolbCWO7aAeiUpW/images/mcp-overview.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=JsolbCWO7aAeiUpW&q=85&s=7219dd88ea643e98069149b149a873ad)

TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import Sandbox from 'e2b'
    
    const sbx = await Sandbox.create({
        mcp: {
            browserbase: {
                apiKey: process.env.BROWSERBASE_API_KEY!,
                geminiApiKey: process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY!,
                projectId: process.env.BROWSERBASE_PROJECT_ID!,
            },
            exa: {
                apiKey: process.env.EXA_API_KEY!,
            },
            airtable: {
                airtableApiKey: process.env.AIRTABLE_API_KEY!,
            },
        },
    });
    
    const mcpUrl = sbx.getMcpUrl();
    const mcpToken = await sbx.getMcpToken();
    
    // You can now connect the gateway to any MCP client, for example claude:
    // This also works for your local claude!
    await sbx.commands.run(`claude mcp add --transport http e2b-mcp-gateway ${mcpUrl} --header "Authorization: Bearer ${mcpToken}"`, { timeoutMs: 0, onStdout: console.log, onStderr: console.log });
    
    await sbx.commands.run(
        `echo 'Use browserbase and exa to research open positions at e2b.dev. Collect your findings in Airtable.' | claude -p --dangerously-skip-permissions`,
        { timeoutMs: 0, onStdout: console.log, onStderr: console.log }
    )
    
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp#documentation)

Filesystem

Get information about a file or directory

You can get information about a file or directory using the `files.getInfo()` / `files.get_info()` methods. Information such as file name, type, and path is returned.

### 

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/info#getting-information-about-a-file)

Getting information about a file

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    
    // Create a new file
    await sandbox.files.write('test_file.txt', 'Hello, world!')
    
    // Get information about the file
    const info = await sandbox.files.getInfo('test_file.txt')
    
    console.log(info)
    // {
    //   name: 'test_file.txt',
    //   type: 'file',
    //   path: '/home/user/test_file.txt',
    //   size: 13,
    //   mode: 0o644, 
    //   permissions: '-rw-r--r--',
    //   owner: 'user',
    //   group: 'user',
    //   modifiedTime: '2025-05-26T12:00:00.000Z',
    //   symlinkTarget: null
    // }
    

### 

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/info#getting-information-about-a-directory)

Getting information about a directory

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    
    // Create a new directory
    await sandbox.files.makeDir('test_dir')
    
    // Get information about the directory
    const info = await sandbox.files.getInfo('test_dir')
    
    console.log(info)
    // {
    //   name: 'test_dir',
    //   type: 'dir',
    //   path: '/home/user/test_dir',
    //   size: 0,
    //   mode: 0o755,
    //   permissions: 'drwxr-xr-x',
    //   owner: 'user',
    //   group: 'user',
    //   modifiedTime: '2025-05-26T12:00:00.000Z',
    //   symlinkTarget: null
    // }

list all running sandboxes

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxID]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#options)

*   `-a, --all: kill all running sandboxes`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

spawn sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.3/sandbox#options-3)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#usage-4)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#usage-5)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.2/template#e2b-template-publish)

*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

work with sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#usage)

    e2b sandbox [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox connect](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-connect)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxID]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all running sandboxes`

[e2b sandbox create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-create)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox create [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#options-4)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.1/sandbox#options-5)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#usage-4)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#usage-5)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.0.6/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

---

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

CopyCopied!

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

unpublish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#usage-7)

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.2/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

---

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/sandbox#usage-3)

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/sandbox#options-4)

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.2/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

CopyCopied!

*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#e2b-template)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#e2b-template-build)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build-v2](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#e2b-template-build-v2)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build-v2 [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
