### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#usage-7)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#e2b-template-publish)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

publish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#usage-8)

    e2b template publish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/template#options-7)

*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[E2B Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=b46f99ca671d766158b23ca43e300829)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=fe02861017e93b6ad520ee0427c429ed)](https://e2b.dev/)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

MCP Gateway

Custom Templates

You can prepull MCP server Docker images during template build time to significantly improve runtime performance.

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-templates#how-it-works)

How it works
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you build a template with prepulled MCP servers, the Docker images for those servers are downloaded and cached during the build process. This means when you create a sandbox from that template, the MCP servers are ready to use immediately without waiting for image downloads.

You must use the MCP gateway enabled template (`mcp-gateway`) as your base template to use this feature.

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-templates#building-a-template-with-mcp-servers)

Building a template with MCP servers
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the `addMcpServer()` method (TypeScript) or `add_mcp_server()` method (Python) to prepull MCP server images during template build. You can pass a single server or an array of servers. The server names (like `"browserbase"` and `"exa"`) correspond to the keys defined in the [Available Servers](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/available-servers)
 documentation.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import "dotenv/config";
    import { Template, defaultBuildLogger } from "e2b";
    
    export const template = Template()
      .fromTemplate("mcp-gateway")
      .addMcpServer(["browserbase", "exa"]);
    
    await Template.build(template, {
      alias: "my-mcp-gateway",
      cpuCount: 8,
      memoryMB: 8192,
      onBuildLogs: defaultBuildLogger(),
    });
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-templates#using-the-template)

Using the template
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once built, create sandboxes from your template alias. You still need to provide the configuration for each MCP server.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from "e2b";
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create({
        template: "my-mcp-gateway",
        mcp: {
            browserbase: {
                apiKey: process.env.BROWSERBASE_API_KEY!,
                geminiApiKey: process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY!,
                projectId: process.env.BROWSERBASE_PROJECT_ID!,
            },
            exa: {
                apiKey: process.env.EXA_API_KEY!,
            },
        },
    });
    
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/mcp/custom-templates#learn-more)

Learn more
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

For more information about working with templates, see:

*   [Template Quickstart](https://e2b.dev/docs/template/quickstart)
     - Get started with custom templates
*   [Defining Templates](https://e2b.dev/docs/template/defining-template)
     - Learn all template configuration options
*   [Template Build](https://e2b.dev/docs/template/build)
     - Understand the build process

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Filesystem

Watch sandbox directory for changes

You can watch a directory for changes using the `files.watchDir()` method in JavaScript and `files.watch_dir()` method in Python.

Since events are tracked asynchronously, their delivery may be delayed. It’s recommended not to collect or close watcher immediately after making a change.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox, FilesystemEventType } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    const dirname = '/home/user'
    
    // Start watching directory for changes
    const handle = await sandbox.files.watchDir(dirname, async (event) => {
      console.log(event)
      if (event.type === FilesystemEventType.WRITE) {
        console.log(`wrote to file ${event.name}`)
      }
    })
    
    // Trigger file write event
    await sandbox.files.write(`${dirname}/my-file`, 'hello')
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/watch#recursive-watching)

Recursive Watching
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can enable recursive watching using the parameter `recursive`.

When rapidly creating new folders (e.g., deeply nested path of folders), events other than `CREATE` might not be emitted. To avoid this behavior, create the required folder structure in advance.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox, FilesystemEventType } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    const dirname = '/home/user'
    
    // Start watching directory for changes
    const handle = await sandbox.files.watchDir(dirname, async (event) => {
      console.log(event)
      if (event.type === FilesystemEventType.WRITE) {
        console.log(`wrote to file ${event.name}`)
      }
    }, {
      recursive: true
    })
    
    // Trigger file write event
    await sandbox.files.write(`${dirname}/my-folder/my-file`, 'hello')
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.0/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.0/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.0/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.0/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.0/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.0/template#e2b-template-list)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.4/template#options)

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.4/template#usage-4)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.4/template#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.4/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.4/template#usage-5)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.3.4/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#usage-8)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/template#options-7)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.0/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.2.0/sandbox#options-3)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

work with sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#usage)

    e2b sandbox [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox connect](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-connect)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`

[e2b sandbox create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-create)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox create [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.1/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

CopyCopied!

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#e2b-template-init)

CopyCopied!

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/template#options-7)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

---

work with sandboxes

    e2b sandbox [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox connect](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-connect)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`

[e2b sandbox create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-create)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CopyCopied!

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.10/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.0.3/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

CopyCopied!

*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox create [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#usage-8)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.1.0/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#usage-3)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#options-2)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#usage-4)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#usage-5)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

[e2b template migrate](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#e2b-template-migrate)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#usage-8)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.2/template#options-7)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.4/template#options-7)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

[e2b template migrate](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.4/template#e2b-template-migrate)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.4/template#usage-9)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.4/template#options-8)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#e2b-template-create)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#usage-2)

    e2b template create [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#usage-4)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#options-3)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#e2b-template-init)

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-n, --name <name>: template name (alias)`
*   `-l, --language <language>: target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`

CopyCopied!

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.0/template#e2b-template-publish)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.5.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.5.1/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.5.1/sandbox#options-3)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v1.4.3/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

---

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#e2b-template-create)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#usage-2)

    e2b template create [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/template#e2b-template-list)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Filesystem

Upload data to sandbox

You can upload data to the sandbox using the `files.write()` method.

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/upload#upload-single-file)

Upload single file
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import fs from 'fs'
    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    
    // Read file from local filesystem
    const content = fs.readFileSync('/local/path')
    // Upload file to sandbox
    await sandbox.files.write('/path/in/sandbox', content)
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/upload#upload-with-pre-signed-url)

Upload with pre-signed URL
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes, you may want to let users from unauthorized environments, like a browser, upload files to the sandbox. For this use case, you can use pre-signed URLs to let users upload files securely. All you need to do is create a sandbox with the `secure: true` option. An upload URL will then be generated with a signature that allows only authorized users to upload files. You can optionally set an expiration time for the URL so that it will be valid only for a limited time.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import fs from 'fs'
    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    // Start a secured sandbox (all operations must be authorized by default)
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create(template, { secure: true })
    
    // Create a pre-signed URL for file upload with a 10 second expiration
    const publicUploadUrl = await sandbox.uploadUrl(
      'demo.txt', {
        useSignatureExpiration: 10_000, // optional
      },
    )
    
    // Upload a file with a pre-signed URL (this can be used in any environment, such as a browser)
    const form = new FormData()
    form.append('file', 'file content')
    
    await fetch(publicUploadUrl, { method: 'POST', body: form })
    
    // File is now available in the sandbox and you can read it
    const content = fs.readFileSync('demo.txt')
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/filesystem/upload#upload-directory-/-multiple-files)

Upload directory / multiple files
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    const fs = require('fs');
    const path = require('path');
    
    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    
    // Read all files in the directory and store their paths and contents in an array
    const readDirectoryFiles = (directoryPath) => {
      // Read all files in the local directory
      const files = fs.readdirSync(directoryPath);
    
      // Map files to objects with path and data
      const filesArray = files
        .filter(file => {
          const fullPath = path.join(directoryPath, file);
          // Skip if it's a directory
          return fs.statSync(fullPath).isFile();
        })
        .map(file => {
          const filePath = path.join(directoryPath, file);
        
          // Read the content of each file
          return {
            path: filePath,
            data: fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8')
          };
        });
    
      return filesArray;
    };
    
    // Usage example
    const files = readDirectoryContents('/local/dir');
    console.log(files); 
    // [\
    //   { path: '/local/dir/file1.txt', data: 'File 1 contents...' },\
    //   { path: '/local/dir/file2.txt', data: 'File 2 contents...' },\
    //   ...\
    // ]
    
    await sandbox.files.write(files)

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.5/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.6/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.6/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.6/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.6/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.6/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.6/template#usage-9)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.6/template#options-8)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

---

[e2b sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

work with sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage)

    e2b sandbox [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox connect](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-connect)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`

[e2b sandbox create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-create)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox create [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#usage-8)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#e2b-template-create)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template create [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#usage-4)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#options-3)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

initialize a new sandbox template using the SDK

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#usage-5)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-n, --name <name>: template name (alias)`
*   `-l, --language <language>: target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#usage-6)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#options-5)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.2/template#e2b-template-publish)

*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#usage-8)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.3/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
