# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-create)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#usage-2)

    e2b template create [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#usage-4)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#options-3)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

initialize a new sandbox template using the SDK

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#usage-5)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-n, --name <name>: template name (alias)`
*   `-l, --language <language>: target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#usage-6)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#options-5)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-publish)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

publish sandbox template

    e2b template publish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#options-7)

*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

[e2b template migrate](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#e2b-template-migrate)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#usage-9)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.1/template#options-8)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

manage sandbox templates

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build-v2](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#e2b-template-build-v2)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build-v2 [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#usage-4)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#options-3)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#usage-6)

    e2b template init-v2 [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#options-5)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-n, --name <name>: template name (alias)`
*   `-l, --language <language>: target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/template#options-9)

*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.8/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# Documentation - E2B

[Skip to main content](https://e2b.dev/docs/quickstart#content-area)

[E2B Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=b46f99ca671d766158b23ca43e300829)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=fe02861017e93b6ad520ee0427c429ed)](https://e2b.dev/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Quickstart

Running your first Sandbox

1

Create E2B account

Every new E2B account get $100 in credits. You can sign up [here](https://e2b.dev/auth/sign-up)
.

2

Set your environment variables

1.  Navigate to the E2B Dashboard.
2.  Copy your API key.
3.  Paste your E2B API key into your .env file.

.env

Copy

Ask AI

    E2B_API_KEY=e2b_***
    

3

Install E2B SDK

Install the E2B SDK to your project by running the following command in your terminal.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    npm i @e2b/code-interpreter dotenv
    

4

Write code for starting Sandbox

We’ll write the minimal code for starting Sandbox, executing Python inside it and listing all files inside the root directory.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    // index.ts
    import 'dotenv/config'
    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sbx = await Sandbox.create() // By default the sandbox is alive for 5 minutes
    const execution = await sbx.runCode('print("hello world")') // Execute Python inside the sandbox
    console.log(execution.logs)
    
    const files = await sbx.files.list('/')
    console.log(files)
    

5

Start your first E2B Sandbox

Run the code with the following command:

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    npx tsx ./index.ts

YesNo

[Raise issue](https://github.com/e2b-dev/docs/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/docs/quickstart)

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build-v2](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-build-v2)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build-v2 [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage-4)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-3)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create basic E2B Dockerfile (./e2b.Dockerfile) in root directory. You can then run e2b template build to build sandbox template from this Dockerfile

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage-5)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

[e2b template init-v2](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-init-v2)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

initialize a new sandbox template using the SDK

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage-6)

    e2b template init-v2 [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-5)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-n, --name <name>: template name (alias)`
*   `-l, --language <language>: target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage-7)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-publish)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-7)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

unpublish sandbox template

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-8)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

[e2b template migrate](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#e2b-template-migrate)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#usage-10)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.9/template#options-9)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`

[e2b sandbox create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-create)

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.3.3/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

[e2b sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

work with sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage)

    e2b sandbox [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox connect](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-connect)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`

[e2b sandbox create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-create)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox create [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#usage-8)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

Legacy Docs

Customize sandbox CPU & RAM

You’re browsing a legacy version of the build system. Visit the [Build System 2.0 documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs/template/quickstart)
.

You can customize the CPU and RAM of your sandbox template via E2B CLI. You’ll need to create a sandbox [template first](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template)
. During the build step, you can specify the CPU and RAM of your sandbox template. The following command will create a sandbox template with 2 CPUs and 2GB of RAM.

Terminal

Copy

Ask AI

    e2b template build -c "/root/.jupyter/start-up.sh" --cpu-count 2 --memory-mb 2048

# Documentation - E2B

[Skip to main content](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#content-area)

[E2B Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=b46f99ca671d766158b23ca43e300829)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=fe02861017e93b6ad520ee0427c429ed)](https://e2b.dev/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Legacy Docs

Sandbox templates

You’re browsing a legacy version of the build system. Visit the [Build System 2.0 documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs/template/quickstart)
.

Sandbox templates allow you to customize the sandbox environment to your needs. To create a sandbox template, you specify the `e2b.Dockerfile`. We then take this Dockerfile and create a new sandbox template from it and give you back a template ID. You can then use this template ID to create a new sandbox with the SDK based on the template you created.

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#how-to-create-custom-sandbox)

How to create custom sandbox
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Steps**

1.  [Install E2B CLI](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#1-install-e2b-cli)
    
2.  [Initialize sandbox template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#2-initialize-sandbox-template)
    
3.  [Customize `e2b.Dockerfile`](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#3-customize-e2b-dockerfile)
    
4.  [Build your sandbox template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#4-build-your-sandbox-template)
    
5.  [Start your custom sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#5-start-your-custom-sandbox)
    

### 

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#1-install-e2b-cli)

1\. Install E2B CLI

**Using Homebrew (on macOS)**

Homebrew

Copy

Ask AI

    brew install e2b
    

**Using NPM**

NPM

Copy

Ask AI

    npm i -g @e2b/cli
    

### 

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#2-initialize-sandbox-template)

2\. Initialize sandbox template

The following command will create a basic `e2b.Dockerfile` in the current directory.

bash

Copy

Ask AI

    e2b template init
    

### 

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#3-customize-e2b-dockerfile)

3\. Customize `e2b.Dockerfile`

Now you can customize your sandbox template by editing the `e2b.Dockerfile` file.

e2b.Dockerfile

Copy

Ask AI

    # Make sure to use this base image
    FROM e2bdev/code-interpreter:latest
    
    # Install some Python packages
    RUN pip install cowsay
    

Only [Debian-based](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Linux_distributions#Debian-based)
 images (e.g., Debian, Ubuntu, or [E2B images](https://hub.docker.com/u/e2bdev)
) are supported.

### 

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#4-build-your-sandbox-template)

4\. Build your sandbox template

Now you can build your sandbox template. We’ll use Docker and the E2B CLI. What is going to happen is that E2B CLI will call Docker to build the image and then push it to the E2B cloud. Then we convert the Docker image to a micro VM that can be then launched as a sandbox with our SDK.

bash

Copy

Ask AI

    e2b template build -c "/root/.jupyter/start-up.sh"
    

This process will take a moment. In the end, you’ll see your template ID that you’ll need to use to create a sandbox with the SDK.

### 

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#5-start-your-custom-sandbox)

5\. Start your custom sandbox

Now you can use the template ID to create a sandbox with the SDK.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    // Your template ID from the previous step
    const templateID = 'id-of-your-template'
    // Pass the template ID to the `Sandbox.create` method
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create(templateID)
    
    // The template installed cowsay, so we can use it
    const execution = await sandbox.runCode(`
    import cowsay
    cowsay.say('Hello from E2B!')
    `)
    
    console.log(execution.stdout)
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#how-it-works)

How it works
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Every time you are building a sandbox template, we create a container based on the [`e2b.Dockerfile`](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template#3-customize-e2b-dockerfile)
 file you create in the process. We extract the container’s filesystem, do provisioning and configuration (e.g. installing required dependencies), and start a sandbox. Then, these steps happen:

1.  We take the running sandbox.
2.  (Only if you specified the [start command](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template/start-cmd)
    , otherwise this step is skipped) Execute the start command.
3.  Wait for readiness (by default 20 seconds if start command is specified, otherwise immediately ready). Readiness check can be configured using [ready command](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox-template/ready-cmd)
    .
4.  Snapshot the sandbox and make it ready for you to spawn it with the SDK.

We call this sandbox snapshot a _sandbox template_.

**Sandbox Snapshot**Snapshots are saved running sandboxes. We serialize and save the whole sandbox’s filesystem together with all the running processes in a way that can be loaded later.This allows us to load the sandbox in a few hundred milliseconds any time later with all the processes already running and the filesystem exactly as it was.

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-create)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-2)

    e2b template create [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-4)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options-3)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

initialize a new sandbox template using the SDK

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-5)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-n, --name <name>: template name (alias)`
*   `-l, --language <language>: target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-6)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options-5)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-publish)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

publish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-7)

    e2b template publish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

unpublish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-8)

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options-7)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

[e2b template migrate](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#e2b-template-migrate)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#usage-9)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.0/template#options-8)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/template#usage-2)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.2.7/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

manage sandbox templates

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#usage-2)

    e2b template create [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#usage-3)

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`

publish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#usage-7)

    e2b template publish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

unpublish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#usage-8)

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#options-7)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

[e2b template migrate](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#e2b-template-migrate)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#usage-9)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/template#options-8)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

work with sandboxes

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage)

    e2b sandbox [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox connect](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-connect)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

connect terminal to already running sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage-2)

    e2b sandbox connect [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b sandbox list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-list)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list all sandboxes, by default it list only running ones

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage-3)

    e2b sandbox list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#options)

*   `-s, --state <state>: filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`
*   `-l, --limit <limit>: limit the number of sandboxes returned`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b sandbox kill](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-kill)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

kill sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage-4)

    e2b sandbox kill [options] [sandboxIDs...]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#options-2)

*   `-a, --all: kill all sandboxes`
*   `-s, --state <state>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by state, eg. running, paused. Defaults to running`
*   `-m, --metadata <metadata>: when used with -a/--all flag, filter by metadata, eg. key1=value1`

[e2b sandbox create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-create)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage-5)

    e2b sandbox create [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#options-3)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox spawn](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-spawn)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

create sandbox and connect terminal to it

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage-6)

    e2b sandbox spawn [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`

[e2b sandbox logs](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-logs)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show logs for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage-7)

    e2b sandbox logs [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#options-5)

*   `--level <level>: filter logs by level (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR). The logs with the higher levels will be also shown. [default: INFO]`
*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming logs until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing logs (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`
*   `--loggers [loggers]: filter logs by loggers. Specify multiple loggers by separating them with a comma.`

[e2b sandbox metrics](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#e2b-sandbox-metrics)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

show metrics for sandbox

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#usage-8)

    e2b sandbox metrics [options] <sandboxID>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.1/sandbox#options-6)

*   `-f, --follow: keep streaming metrics until the sandbox is closed`
*   `--format <format>: specify format for printing metrics (json, pretty) [default: pretty]`

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[e2b template](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

manage sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage)

    e2b template [options] [command]
    

CopyCopied!

[e2b template create](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-create)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build Dockerfile as a Sandbox template. This command reads a Dockerfile and builds it directly.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-2)

    e2b template create [options] <template-name>
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template build](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-build)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

build sandbox template defined by ./e2b.Dockerfile or ./Dockerfile in root directory. By default the root directory is the current working directory. This command also creates e2b.toml config.

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-3)

    e2b template build [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options-2)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. By default E2B tries to find e2b.Dockerfile or Dockerfile in root directory.`
*   `-n, --name <template-name>: specify sandbox template name. You can use the template name to start the sandbox with SDK. The template name must be lowercase and contain only letters, numbers, dashes and underscores.`
*   `-c, --cmd <start-command>: specify command that will be executed when the sandbox is started.`
*   `--ready-cmd <ready-command>: specify command that will need to exit 0 for the template to be ready.`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `--cpu-count <cpu-count>: specify the number of CPUs that will be used to run the sandbox. The default value is 2.`
*   `--memory-mb <memory-mb>: specify the amount of memory in megabytes that will be used to run the sandbox. Must be an even number. The default value is 512.`
*   `--build-arg <args...>: specify additional build arguments for the build command. The format should be <varname>=<value>.`
*   `--no-cache: skip cache when building the template.`

[e2b template list](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

list sandbox templates

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-4)

    e2b template list [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options-3)

*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-f, --format <format>: output format, eg. json, pretty`

[e2b template init](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-init)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

initialize a new sandbox template using the SDK

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-5)

    e2b template init [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options-4)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `-n, --name <name>: template name (alias)`
*   `-l, --language <language>: target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`

[e2b template delete](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-delete)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

delete sandbox template and e2b.toml config

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-6)

    e2b template delete [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options-5)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual delete confirmation`

[e2b template publish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-publish)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

publish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-7)

    e2b template publish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options-6)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual publish confirmation`

[e2b template unpublish](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-unpublish)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

unpublish sandbox template

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-8)

    e2b template unpublish [options] [template]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options-7)

*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-s, --select: select sandbox template from interactive list`
*   `-t, --team <team-id>: specify the team ID that the operation will be associated with. You can find team ID in the team settings in the E2B dashboard (https://e2b.dev/dashboard?tab=team).`
*   `-y, --yes: skip manual unpublish confirmation`

[e2b template migrate](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#e2b-template-migrate)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

migrate e2b.Dockerfile and e2b.toml to new Template SDK format

### [Usage](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#usage-9)

    e2b template migrate [options]
    

CopyCopied!

### [Options](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/cli/v2.4.2/template#options-8)

*   `-d, --dockerfile <file>: specify path to Dockerfile. Defaults to e2b.Dockerfile`
*   `--config <e2b-toml>: specify path to the E2B config toml. By default E2B tries to find ./e2b.toml in root directory.`
*   `-l, --language <language>: specify target language: typescript, python-sync, python-async`
*   `-p, --path <path>: change root directory where command is executed to <path> directory`

# Documentation - E2B

[Skip to main content](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox/metadata#content-area)

[E2B Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=b46f99ca671d766158b23ca43e300829)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/e2b/pduSmNOyhS35xRWk/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=pduSmNOyhS35xRWk&q=85&s=fe02861017e93b6ad520ee0427c429ed)](https://e2b.dev/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Sandbox

Sandbox metadata

Metadata is a way to attach arbitrary key-value pairs for a sandbox. This is useful in various scenarios, for example:

*   Associate a sandbox with a user session.
*   Store custom user data for a sandbox like API keys.
*   Associate a sandbox with a user ID and [connect to it later](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox/connect)
    .

You specify metadata when creating a sandbox and can access it later through listing running sandboxes with `Sandbox.list()` method.

JavaScript & TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    // Create sandbox with metadata.
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create({
      metadata: {
        userId: '123',
      },
    })
    
    // List running sandboxes and access metadata.
    const runningSandboxes = await Sandbox.list()
    // Will print:
    // {
    //   'userId': '123',
    // }
    console.log(runningSandboxes[0].metadata)
    

[​](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox/metadata#filtering-sandboxes-by-metadata)

Filtering sandboxes by metadata
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also filter sandboxes by metadata, you can find more about it [here](https://e2b.dev/docs/sandbox/list#filtering-sandboxes)
.

# SDK Reference - E2B

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

[](https://e2b.dev/)

[Documentation](https://e2b.dev/docs)

### [Sandbox](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/code-interpreter-js-sdk/v1.0.4/sandbox#sandbox)

E2B cloud sandbox is a secure and isolated cloud environment.

The sandbox allows you to:

*   Access Linux OS
*   Create, list, and delete files and directories
*   Run commands
*   Run isolated code
*   Access the internet

Check docs here.

Use Sandbox.create to create a new sandbox.

#### Example

    import { Sandbox } from '@e2b/code-interpreter'
    
    const sandbox = await Sandbox.create()
    

CopyCopied!

#### Methods

### [createCodeContext()](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/code-interpreter-js-sdk/v1.0.4/sandbox#create-code-context)

    createCodeContext(opts?: CreateCodeContextOpts): Promise<Context>
    

CopyCopied!

Creates a new context to run code in.

###### Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `opts`? | `CreateCodeContextOpts` | options for creating the context. |

###### Returns

`Promise`<`Context`\>

context object.

### [runCode()](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/code-interpreter-js-sdk/v1.0.4/sandbox#run-code)

###### runCode(code, opts)

    runCode(code: string, opts?: RunCodeOpts & object): Promise<Execution>
    

CopyCopied!

Run the code as Python.

Specify the `language` or `context` option to run the code as a different language or in a different `Context`.

You can reference previously defined variables, imports, and functions in the code.

###### Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `code` | `string` | code to execute. |
| `opts`? | `RunCodeOpts` & `object` | options for executing the code. |

###### Returns

`Promise`<`Execution`\>

`Execution` result object.

###### runCode(code, opts)

    runCode(code: string, opts?: RunCodeOpts & object): Promise<Execution>
    

CopyCopied!

Run the code for the specified language.

Specify the `language` or `context` option to run the code as a different language or in a different `Context`. If no language is specified, Python is used.

You can reference previously defined variables, imports, and functions in the code.

###### Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `code` | `string` | code to execute. |
| `opts`? | `RunCodeOpts` & `object` | options for executing the code. |

###### Returns

`Promise`<`Execution`\>

`Execution` result object.

###### runCode(code, opts)

    runCode(code: string, opts?: RunCodeOpts & object): Promise<Execution>
    

CopyCopied!

Runs the code in the specified context, if not specified, the default context is used.

Specify the `language` or `context` option to run the code as a different language or in a different `Context`.

You can reference previously defined variables, imports, and functions in the code.

###### Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `code` | `string` | code to execute. |
| `opts`? | `RunCodeOpts` & `object` | options for executing the code |

###### Returns

`Promise`<`Execution`\>

`Execution` result object

[Interfaces](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/code-interpreter-js-sdk/v1.0.4/sandbox#interfaces)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CopyCopied!

###### Default

### [Context](https://e2b.dev/docs/sdk-reference/code-interpreter-js-sdk/v1.1.1/sandbox#context)

    type Context: object;
    

CopyCopied!

Represents a context for code execution.

#### Type declaration

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `cwd` | `string` | The working directory of the context. |
| `id` | `string` | The ID of the context. |
| `language` | `string` | The language of the context. |
